shouldn't get ourselves in a situation like the one we just had. <br>
Take it easy. If we need help, we must organize it. We accepted the fact that this was going to cost us money. So be it.<br>
<br>
The track went downhill from here. As soon as we hit the valley we could
 not get up a stupid little hill. The front wheels were spinning wildly.
 <br>
<br>
Right! <br>
<br>
We talked to the guys who were looking at our ridiculous attempts of 
climbing this ridiculous koppie. They gave us a friendly impression. We 
explained our situation, our broken diff, etc... We stressed the fact 
that we were not working for some corporation or NGO. We did not have 
the budgets these corporations have. We mentioned that we were willing 
to pay for help, but not much. It's not because we are mundeles that we 
would pay them insance amounts of money.<br>
<br>
Our reasoning was that if they started a discussion at this point in 
time already, that they would cause us a lot of trouble later on. But 
they agreed. They wanted to help us and work at a 'normal' rate. We 
'hired' three guys. Vita, Mufuta and 'papa' Bazil. They were overly 
optimistic and said we would reach Kapia that same evening!<br>
<br>
Kapia is the village where this track joins the 'Belgian' road.</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">The
 main job of our 'crew' was to flatten the road as much as possible. And
 give us a push if we couldn't get over things. They would level the 
road, 50 meters at a time and then we would drive as far as we could, 
etc.. etc..<br>
<br>
This was actually working rather well! My depression from earlier that day was already forgotten! <br>
<br>
Imagine you are walking on the street, minding your own business. And 
some chap comes up and explains he has a problem. He asks you for help. 
You agree and travel with him to his destination. You have no idea who 
this guy is. You have no idea when you will go home again. You did not 
inform your family that you would probably not come home that night.<br>
That is how we recruited Mufuta, Basil and Vita.<br>
<br>
They were an energetic bunch and did their work with a lot of 
enthousiasm. Cheering and singing when we had gotten trough another 
'obstacle'. They were proud of their task too, and explained it to all 
the people we passed. We often had a few extra helping hands. <br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-1-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-1-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-1-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/dibaya018.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya018.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/dibaya018.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
L'office des routes from Congo actually owes us a lot of money as we were reconstructing the roads!<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-2-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-2-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-2-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/dibaya017.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya017.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/dibaya017.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-3-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-3-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-3-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/dibaya015.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya015.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/dibaya015.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-4-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-4-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-4-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/dibaya016.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya016.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/dibaya016.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper"><div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-5-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-5-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-5-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya008.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya008.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya008.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
After a few hours, the enthousiasm wore off from our crew. They too 
started to realize that this was very though and slow going. The road 
hadn't improved either. Especially Basil, who was already a bit older, 
was getting tired. By the time we reached a looong hill we were barely 
moving again. <br>
<br>
The group of people that was following us grew larger and larger. But 
they were not helping with the digging. They occasionally helped with 
the pushing. This was partly because of Mufuta, Basil and Vita had told 
them they alone were allowed to help. This to secure their fee. At 
least, that is what we guessed... they talked Lingala to eachother. We 
had also told them upfront that we would pay for 3 guys, not an entire 
village! We are not quite sure how, but after a while other people 
started helping. Did our 'crew' tell them they would share their fee? Or
 did they just help because they wanted to?<br>
<br>
I don't know... but we could really need the help. We were running in the last hours of daylight again. <br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-6-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-6-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-6-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya009.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya009.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya009.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-7-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-7-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-7-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya013.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya013.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya013.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-8-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-8-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-8-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya014.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya014.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya014.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">We had removed our spare wheels. This allowed more people to push. <br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-9-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-9-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-9-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya012.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya012.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya012.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-10-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-10-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-10-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya011.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya011.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya011.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
The later it got, the more people arrived. And the louder everybody got.
 Our 'crew' had by now grown to 20 something strong guys. they only had 3
 shovels, but they worked in teams. And as soon a piece of road was 
'ready' they all gathered behind our Landcruiser and pushed. They sang 
working songs to give the pace. People were clapping in their hands. 
Every 5 meter we progressed was a reason to celebrate. People cheered 
and dansed. <br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-11-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-11-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-11-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya020.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya020.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya020.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-12-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-12-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-12-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya021.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya021.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya021.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-13-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-13-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-13-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya022.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya022.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya022.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-14-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-14-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-14-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya023.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya023.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya023.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper"><div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-15-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-15-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-15-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya025.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya025.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya025.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
I cannot help myself from moving rythmically behind my keyboard whilst 
typing this when I think about the ambiance. You could see people going 
completely wild of excitement everytime we kicked up mud with our 
spinning tyres while slowly creeping forward. I could feel the trusts at
 the back of the car from the pushing people. This hill was steep and 
the ruts were bad. Most people helping us now were from the next 
village. They had a vision, they wanted to get us in their village for 
the night!<br>
<br>
It was sometimes though, but they kept their - and our - spirits up.<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-16-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-16-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-16-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya026.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya026.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya026.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-17-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-17-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-17-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya030.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya030.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya030.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-18-1587032712" data-lb-id="_xfUid-18-1587032712">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-18-1587032712" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya027.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya027_002.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya027.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">When we reached the top of the 
hill everybody was going nuts. So were we! We couldn't believe we had 
actually gotten up here with a broken rear axle. That was some seriosuly
 difficult terrain!<br>
It was a now few hundred meters downhill and people climbed on our 
roofrack and hung on our doors for the ride. We were too enthousiastic 
to say anything about it now.<br>
<br>
We could stay next to Papa Likas's house. He was the guy who took the 
lead in the last climb. A somewhat older guy, and clearly one of the 
'richer' people in the village. He might have lacked the degrees and the
 education, but we could tell he was a clever and wise man. We were 
offered two chairs (funny how this form of politeness exists everywhere 
in congo). They were very funny affairs, huge thrones made out of heavy 
wood. We felt like the king and the queen. <br>
<br>
We were offered food - foufou and some fish - but we politely refused. 
It looked ok, but we did not want to risk getting ill now. We were too 
weak already (Josephine still had serious stomach problems). As usual we
 could see the people were actually happy that we did not eat, they 
didn't have too much.<br>
<br>
Our supply of water was low again. The 20 liters that had cost me so 
much energy yesterday was almost gone. Very, very carefully we inquired 
if they had a water supply. There was indeed a source, but "c'est très 
loin" - "it is very far". When he says it is far, I believe him! They 
bring us a small supply of rainwater to freshen us up. We will have to 
ration our remaing water.<br>
<br>
It struck me how difficult it is to get water here. People would have to
 walk hours and hours to reach a source. While at the same time the 
forest is so humid and sticky.<br>
<br>
I checked the GPS. We had moved no more then 5km today. I had reached my
 limit today. Although I felt ok now, I could feel that I did not have 
any more reserves. Josephine was the hero of the day, without a doubt. 
But she was suffering from her stomach problems. <br>
<br>
The village had become quiet again. Darkness had hidden the little huts 
in the forest. People could be seen, gathered around little fires. We 
saw a larger group of people gathered around hut. A strange kind of 
singing could be heard.. a very sad and mysterious sound. Papa Likas 
explained that a child was very ill and did not have long to live. 
People were praying. When asked what illness the child had, Papa Likas 
replied "On ne sait pas" - "We don't know". There are no doctors here.  
Another child from the same family died last month.<br>
<br>
We had a great evening with dancing and singing and all looked good and 
fine. And then Congo slaps us in the face again with its hard reality.</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">Progress
 after day 23 on the road. Day 28 since we entered DRC. I did not bother
 trying to add our progress on the map. The scale of the map does not 
allow for such small markings  :roll: <br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-1-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-1-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-1-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/congo_democratic_republic_map-day22.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/congo_democratic_republic_map-day22.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/congo_democratic_republic_map-day22.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper"><blockquote class="bbCodeBlock bbCodeBlock--expandable bbCodeBlock--quote">
	
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-title">
			
				<a href="file:///forum/goto/post?id=745174" class="bbCodeBlock-sourceJump" data-xf-click="attribution" data-content-selector="#post-745174">LaOutbackTrail said:</a>
			
		</div>
	
	<div class="bbCodeBlock-content">
		
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-expandContent ">
			I know the heat stroke thing sucks.<br>
...<br>
Did you have any permanent effects from your situation?
		</div>
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-expandLink"><a>Click to expand...</a></div>
	</div>
</blockquote>No, it was a minor heatstroke combined with fatigue. I felt
 really bad for a few hours, but quickly recovered. Adrenaline is a good
 medicine ;-) Until then I had a seemingly neverending strength and 
endurance. I lost it then, I got tired very quickly from physical work 
from that moment on. But nothing permanent.<br>
<br>
Having it whilst riding a bike must be a very scary experience!</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper"><b>Day 24</b><br>
<br>
I really had to force myself out of our tent that morning, despite the 
noise off the village. My muscles hurt and my eyes preferred to stay 
closed.<br>
<br>
Mufuta, Vita and papa Basil had returned to their own village for the 
night, but they would come back. We sat down with papa Likas. He offered
 his help and we gave him the same explenation we gave earlier to the 
first members of our crew. He agreed with the conditions. He suggested 
we 'hire' 5 extra guys, including him, from his village. We knew we 
needed that kind of manpower to push 4 ton of Toyota trough the jungle. 
They would join us until we reach Kapia. Apparantely the road there is 
much better and we would be able to drive on our own to Dibaya-Lubwe 
from there.<br>
<br>
Papa likas made a drawing of how the road went all the way to Kapia. The
 first few kilometer would be slightly downhill until we reached a 
river. From there the road was uphill all the way to Kapia. The first 
part of the hill would be the hardest as this was in a forest with the 
usual ruts. Halfway to the top the road leaves the forest and we would 
be in much easier savannah.<br>
<br>
"Nous allons y arriver avant midi!" - "we will get there (Kapia) before noon"<br>
<br>
As soon as Mufuta, Basil and Vita arrived we were on the road again. Our
 batteries were now officially dead so we needed a push to get started. 
It was key not to turn of the engine now! Our crew loved the raw sound 
of our broken exhaust!<br>
<br>
We advanced quickly. Our crew was hanging on the sides of the car while 
two guys were walking in front, making quick improvements along the way.
 The way we progressed our first few hundred meters made mea actually 
believe we would make it to Kapie before noon! We must be the two most 
naive people in the world!<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-2-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-2-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-2-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya032.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya032.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya032.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-3-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-3-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-3-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya034.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya034.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya034.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
It had been a while since we saw serious rain. Frequent showers yes, but
 not cloud bursts. Until now. Just when we arrived at the river in the 
bottom of the valley fat raindrops were falling from the sky. This 
usually means trouble. Our crew searched for cover in the forest while 
we sat in our car whilst a could emptied itself violently right on top 
of us. We could see the mostly dry road transform in a muddy stream. The
 hard compressed mud was gleaming.</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">(This post is not part of the report)<br>
<br>
I just read the latest UN report on human development (<a href="http://hdr.undp.org/en/" target="_blank" class="link link--external" data-proxy-href="/forum/proxy.php?link=http%3A%2F%2Fhdr.undp.org%2Fen%2F&amp;hash=2da1b559c1ab9e7ba81cc66f62da0adb" rel="nofollow noopener">http://hdr.undp.org/en/</a>). It's interesting:<br>
<br>




<blockquote class="bbCodeBlock bbCodeBlock--expandable bbCodeBlock--quote">
	
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-title">
			
				UN - Human Development Report 2010 said:
			
		</div>
	
	<div class="bbCodeBlock-content">
		
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-expandContent ">
			The UN Development Programme's report concludes that since 1970 there
 has been significant progress - often underestimated until now - and 
that the fastest progress has been in some of the poorest countries.
		</div>
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-expandLink"><a>Click to expand...</a></div>
	</div>
</blockquote>



<blockquote class="bbCodeBlock bbCodeBlock--expandable bbCodeBlock--quote">
	
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-title">
			
				UN - Human Development Report 2010 said:
			
		</div>
	
	<div class="bbCodeBlock-content">
		
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-expandContent ">
			In Africa only three countries have gone backwards since 1970 - the 
Democratic Republic of Congo, Zimbabwe and Zambia - the first two 
because of conflict and bad government, and the last principally because
 of HIV/Aids.
		</div>
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-expandLink"><a>Click to expand...</a></div>
	</div>
</blockquote>And it is not like it was going that well with DRC in 1970 :-(<br>
<br>
Source: <a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-11694599" target="_blank" class="link link--external" data-proxy-href="/forum/proxy.php?link=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.bbc.co.uk%2Fnews%2Fworld-11694599&amp;hash=237440c100ff914ae39ff9598a9f7794" rel="nofollow noopener">http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-11694599</a></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper"><div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-4-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-4-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-4-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya035.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya035.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya035.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
This rain couldn't have come in a worse time. The road was now extra 
slippery and we already struggled so much with grip - or the lack 
thereof. Our crew worked hard to construct a road that would provide us 
an as level as possible path with as much grip as possible. It took a 
huge amount of energy for every meter we worked ourselves forward.<br>
<br>
We could see our crew was losing its motivation and we feared that they 
would just give up or demand more money. It was Josephine that 
discovered the magic of our camera. These guys loved the camera! 
Everytime the camera came out they posed and they work like crazy to 
look cool on the pictures.<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-5-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-5-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-5-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya037.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya037.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya037.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
I stalled the engine. I felt really bad about it as they could not 
pushstart us uphill. Only downhill. I let the Landcruiser roll backwards
 for a few meters and it still wouldn't start. The lost few meters would
 cost us hours to get up again. I did not want to go backwards any 
longer. So while our crew continued clearing the road,  I started to get
 our auxiliary batteries out again. <br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-6-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-6-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-6-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya041.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya041.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya041.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-7-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-7-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-7-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya040.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya040.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya040.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
Everything was just so hard now. Getting the engine started again had 
cost us an hour. The original enthousiasm was completely gone, we were 
moving forward at a rate of a meter per hour. The hill was about 
700meters long.<br>
<br>
We stopped progressing at all when we had to go trough a small detour around a tree. It was small but steep incline.<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-8-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-8-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-8-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya044.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya044.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya044.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-9-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-9-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-9-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya042.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya042.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya042.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper"><div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-10-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-10-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-10-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya043.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya043.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya043.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
With the rain also came the little moisture flies. Millions of them. 
tiny little flies. They favoured our eyes and ears and loved our nose. 
Annoying little thingies!<br>
<br>
We tried everything to make the road better in order toget us up this 
little hill. We had at least 10 attempts to climb it, but it just didn't
 work. <br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-11-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-11-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-11-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya048.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya048.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya048.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-12-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-12-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-12-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya051.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya051.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya051.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
Since we left the village early this morning we had covered 4 kilometer.
 Of which the first 3,8km were done in the first two hours. The rest of 
the day we spent on this hill. The last 3 hours we hadn't moved at all.<br>
<br>
Darkness was setting in again, we weren't going anywhere today..<br>
<br>
The crew wanted to return to their village for the night. We would be 
camping here. Just when our guys wanted to leave the news came that the 
sick child in the last village had died. A messenger was sent to the 
surrounding villages. This meant a lot of people would want to visit the
 family of the kid, so there will be a lot of traffic on the roads that 
night. A creepy thought to be camping spot in the middle of this 
situation, all alone on the Congolese jungle.<br>
<br>
Kapia became a mythic place for us. Our own Atlantis. The hidden city 
that nobody knew where it was. We started having our doubts if we would 
ever get our car out of this jungle again. Tomorrow is another day..<br>
<br>
We opened our tent in the place where we were stuck. All the batteries 
from our flashlights were empty (from last nights rythmic struggle) so 
we helped ourselves with a candle. The rainforest was insanely loud and 
peaceful at the same time. I would have loved this place otherwise, but 
it was hard to forget in what kind of trouble we were.</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">Progress after day 24... Day 29 since we entered Congo.<br>
None at all really... Camping in the jungle<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-13-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-13-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-13-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/congo_democratic_republic_map-day22.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/congo_democratic_republic_map-day22.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/congo_democratic_republic_map-day22.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper"><b>Day 25</b><br>
<br>
Our 30th day since we entered Congo. That needs to be celebrated! But 
not with any drinking. We are out of drinking water. It had rained a lot
 that night and our tent was still leaking.<br>
<br>
We had given an emtpy water jerrycan with papa Likas last night and he 
said he'd return with a full one today. But what we were mostly looking 
out for was that tirfor he was talking about. They knew, that a guy in 
their village used to have a tirfor, but they had not seen it in the 
last years. Likas would try to trace it down.<br>
<br>
We were delighted to see our crew again, not only with a full jerrycan 
of water, but also with a tirfor! But it didn't come for free..  :roll: 
The owner wanted 50$US to 'rent' the tirfor. This was an odd situation 
as we did not agree with that price, but the owners was not here to 
discuss it with him. We decided we would be wanting to spend 15$US - 
which is a lot of money! - and papa Likas thought that the owner would 
agree with that. <br>
<br>
I had already taken the auxiliary batteries out again early in the 
morning, so we could immediately start the engine and try to finally get
 out of this pit!<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-14-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-14-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-14-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya049.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya049.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya049.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-15-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-15-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-15-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya054.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya054.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya054.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
It worked!! This was a big morale booster. A booster we desperately needed! <br>
Likas and Mufuta were delighted too<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-16-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-16-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-16-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya057.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya057.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya057.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">Centimeter after centimer we 
creeped forward. This was faster moving then what we managed yesterday! 
Even if it was going so slowly, the psychological effect cannot be 
underestimated. The previous days we would be be digging for hours after
 which we blasted forward for 50 meters and then had to start digging 
again. That is pretty depressing.<br>
But now we were constantly moving, incredibly slow, but every 5 minutes you could see progress was being made.<br>
<br>
It was hard work though. Our crew did a great job!<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-17-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-17-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-17-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya060.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya060.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya060.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-18-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-18-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-18-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya061.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya061.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya061.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-19-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-19-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-19-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya062.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya062.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya062.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-20-1587032723" data-lb-id="_xfUid-20-1587032723">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-20-1587032723" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya067.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya067.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya067.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">Because of our involvement with 
our 'crew' we did not have too much trouble with the begging here. Apart
 from that I believe we had been very lucky to break down here.<br>
<br>
:scratch: <br>
<br>
Let's rephrase that last sentence: "We could have broken down in a much 
worse region then this, people were generally nice around here."<br>
<br>
By now we had become part of the road. Early in the morning we had the 
kids that passed trough. They were very curious but they could not stay 
long as they had to go to school. You could see the dilemma on their 
faces, every fibre of their body wanted to stay around and check out 
these white guys, but they would get into serious trouble if they did 
not show up in school!<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-1-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-1-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-1-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya059.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya059.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya059.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
We felt sorry for the bike transporters that had to pass trough here. 
They had such a hard task at hands already, and then we created an extra
 obstacle by blocking the road with out truck. <br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-2-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-2-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-2-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya064.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya064.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya064.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-3-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-3-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-3-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya065.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya065.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya065.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-4-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-4-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-4-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya058.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya058.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya058.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">After the little detour there 
was a short level piece of track before going steep uphil again. I took 
as much run-up as possible and launched myself up the hill. This won us 
20 meters or so.<br>
<br>
Josephine: "What was that noise?"<br>
Me: "What noise?"<br>
Josephine: "That tak-tak noise?"<br>
Me: "Don't know"<br>
<br>
I had heard the noise too but I did not want to think or worry about it. Not now.<br>
<br>
The road was too steep to even attempt driving up with our front axle 
alone. We would use the tirfor for the remaining 500m. The length of the
 cable gave us about 10meter of progress with each go. Then the tirfor 
had to be released and a new tree had to be found to continue. 500 
meters. 10 meter at a time. Everybody knew this was going to be a big 
job. But once we would make it open we would be out of the forest and 
onto the savannah, were it would be possible to drive on our own steam 
again. That was a big motivation.<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-5-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-5-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-5-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya066.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya066.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya066.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-6-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-6-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-6-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya068.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya068.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya068.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-7-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-7-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-7-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya069.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya069.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya069.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
My respect for these guys is endless. It is incredible how they could 
manage such hard labour for hours on end. If the motivation got low, the
 camera always cheered them up again. They barely eat or drink. At this 
rate I would have died already... twice.<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-8-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-8-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-8-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya072.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya072.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya072.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
This last pictures gives and idea of the angle we were working at.<br>
<br>
"Tonight we would surely reach Kapia!"</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">The
 guys were getting hungry. We could not blame them. They did not have 
food, and the nearest village was 5km behind us. Our food stock was low 
too, but we still had porridge. We bought a lot of porridge as it is 
very nutritious and takes little space in the car. I don't like porridge
 very much but we had eaten it every day since we were on the road.<br>
<br>
We cooked up a big pot for them. They loved it. To make it a bit tastier
 we gave them our pot of sugar, so they could add a bit to their 
porridge. We were still cleaning up our cooking gear and by the time we 
returned the sugar was all gone. They just ate a full kilogram of pure 
sugar! <br>
<br>
About halfway up the hill we ran out of trees. The trees had made way 
for thick bush. But nothing strong enough to hook up the tirfor...  
:scratch: <br>
Nothing is easy in Congo.. We cut down a tree.<br>
<br>
The procedure for the last 250meters changed a bit:<br>
<br>
Dig a deep hole in the middle of the road. Put the tree in the hole. 
Close the hole. Attach the tirfor and winch the Landcruiser 10meters 
forward. Dig out the tree. Close the hole. 10meters further, dig a deep 
hole in the middle of the road... And repeat.<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-9-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-9-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-9-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya075.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya075.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya075.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-10-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-10-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-10-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya076.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya076.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya076.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-11-1587032734" data-lb-id="_xfUid-11-1587032734">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-11-1587032734" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya077.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya077.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya077.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">When we just started with the 
tirfor that morning everybody was optimistic. Kapia seemed so close by. 
Everybody worked extremely hard for 10 hours non-stop and we had only 
progressed 500meters. So mouch trouble for so little result. We still 
hadn't mae it up the hill and out of the forest, although we were close 
now.<br>
<br>
It got dark again.<br>
<br>
Nobody wanted to stop now, you could tell from everybody's face how 
tired they were. Papa Bazil started a song and the work continued. 
Everybody sang. No more joking, no more pausing. Just working at a 
steady pace to get this damn Landcruiser on top of the hill.<br>
<br>
Papa Likas told me it was his greatest wish to hop on to the back of our
 car when we made it to top and ride together with us to Kapia. There 
his task would end and would finally be able to go home to his family. 
We shared his wish!<br>
<br>
Late in the evening we made to the top, I still had the engine running since this morning. We were nervous.<br>
<br>
I put it in 1st and let the clutch go. We moved!<br>
<br>
*TAK*TAK*TAK*</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">Everybody was shaking. Our helpers because of all the sugar they ate. We from anxiety.<br>
<br>
Who were we kidding anyway. We had heard the tak-tak sound before and we
 knew what it meant. I guess we were just hoping it would have been a 
dry birfield or something. Whishfull thinking.<br>
<br>
A quick run trough the the front driveline components showed the the 
noise came from inside the front differential. Trying to drive now only 
resulted in noise, no more movement. <br>
<br>
Our front diff had completely packed up. <br>
<br>
We switched the engine off and it became silent. Very silent. You could 
see the dissapointment on the faces of our crew. We had a deal with 
them, they would bring us to Kapia, no matter what, and we would pay 
them for the service. They were afraid now that they would not get paid 
(or paid less) as we would obviously not reach Kapia.<br>
<br>
We had to decide very quickly how and how much we would pay.  This is so
 difficult! We had no idea what a reasonable amount would be. We did not
 want to pay them too little. Because they deserved an honest wage and 
we certainly did not want to make enemies here. On the other hand we did
 not want to pay them to much as that would only open the doors for 
corruption and create the impression that 'white people' always pay too 
much.<br>
<br>
We decided on 150$US for all of them. 150$US divided by 8 = 19$US per 
person. For three very long had working days. Josephine asked me if I 
would be happy with that amount? I wouldn't. I'd feel insulted and angry
 probably. But in Congo that is a lot of money. This was so difficult!<br>
<br>
We gave the money to papa Likas and thanked them for all their work. We 
also gave them our axe, for which they were very grateful. We barely 
used it anyway. <br>
<br>
Our crew then dissapeared in the darkness, leaving us all alone on the savannah.<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-3-1587032745" data-lb-id="_xfUid-3-1587032745">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-3-1587032745" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya079.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/dibaya079.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/550/dibaya079.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div>

<br>
<br>
<br>
Papa Bazil, Mufuta, Vita, Papa Likas, Masambe, Bony <br>
<br>
We knew we had a bit of problem here, but we did not discuss it too 
much. We were tired and hungry. There is nothing we could do now anyway 
so we opened up our tent and made ourselves a nice meal. We cooked some 
pasta, opened a can of tuna and used our last package of instant 
mushroom sauce. Whatever would happen tomorrow, we might as wel do it 
well fed.<br>
<br>
20 minutes after our crew had left we heard some very loud "YAHOO's" 
emerging from the forest. We recognized the voices. Probably they had 
waited with counting the money until now, and the result seemed to make 
them very happy. We paid too much..<br>
<br>
It was a beautiful night again, as we were in the savannah now we had a 
clear view of the sky. The African sky can be so magnificently 
beautiful. We only had a candle to provide us with some light. In 
different situations this would have been the perfect bushcamp.<br>
<br>
A strange sense of rest came over us, in a way we felt relieved. We were
 happy that we would no longer have to struggle with only a functional  
front axle.</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">Progress after day 25 on the road. Our 30th day in DRC.<br>
These progress report are becoming useless really, as we had not really progressed today (700meter)<br>
<br>


	
	
		
		
	


	<div class="lbContainer lbContainer--inline " title="" data-xf-init="lightbox" data-lb-single-image="1" data-lb-container-zoom="1" data-lb-trigger=".js-lbImage-_xfUid-4-1587032745" data-lb-id="_xfUid-4-1587032745">
		
			<div class="lbContainer-zoomer js-lbImage-_xfUid-4-1587032745" data-src="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/congo_democratic_republic_map-day22.jpg" aria-label="Zoom"></div>
		
		<img src="congo_files/congo_democratic_republic_map-day22.jpg" data-url="http://radiobaobab.be/assets/etogal/549/congo_democratic_republic_map-day22.jpg" class="bbImage" data-zoom-target="1" alt="" style="">
	</div></div><hr><div class="bbWrapper"><b>Day 26</b><br>
<br>
We slept until the heat of the sun chased us out of our tent and cooked up a strong breakfast of my <i>favourite</i> porridge.<br>
<br>
It was time for a sitwrap:<br>
<br>
- Our car's bodywork was badly damaged<br>
- Exhaust broken off<br>
- Two broken batteries<br>
- Rear drivetrain broken<br>
- Front drivertrain broken<br>
- Our gearbox was no longer connected in to our wheels = not possible to jumpstart. Not possible to move.<br>
- Running low on food<br>
- Running very low on water, less then 2 liters.<br>
- Nobody knew where we were. The last time we were able to contact somebody was in Kananga. 2 weeks ago.<br>
- No cell phone reception.<br>
<br>
We hid all valuable things (camera, GPS, ..) in our car.<br>
We left a note inside our car with a description of our intentions.<br>
We blinded the windows as good as we could.<br>
We put on our hiking boots and a hat.<br>
We took our passports, our 2 mobile phones, some immodium and dafalgan and some sunscreen.<br>
We filled a bottle with our last remaining bit of water.<br>
We locked the doors of our car<br>
<br>
We walked out...</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper">For the record: this is not over yet <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" class="smilie smilie--sprite smilie--sprite1" alt=":)" title="Smile    :)" data-shortname=":)"><br>
<br>
We were on a 2 year trip, of which this Congo bit is just a very small 
part. We had sold everything we owned in order to be able to do this 
trip. The car and its content were (and you can take that very 
literally) the only things we owned. There was no house at home, no 
furniture, no clothes. As a matter of fact, there was no 'at home' other
 then our Landcruiser. And indeed, we had a carnet on this car. We were 
not just going to leave it there. <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" class="smilie smilie--sprite smilie--sprite1" alt=":)" title="Smile    :)" data-shortname=":)"><br>
<br>
As for the dureability of the car: I will post my afterthoughts when the
 report is finished. Let's just not forget that we were already 
travelling 20 months non-stop. We had already completed 2 trans-africa's
 and a trans-asia. 95% offroad, some of it pretty extreme. A lot more 
gory technical details and insights will come in the next few 
installments.<br>
<br>
Apologies for not providing this perspective any earlier.</div><hr><div class="bbWrapper"><blockquote class="bbCodeBlock bbCodeBlock--expandable bbCodeBlock--quote">
	
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-title">

		</div>
	
	<div class="bbCodeBlock-content">
		
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-expandContent ">
			Sure, but who could take it?  Should we send him back for part two?
		</div>
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-expandLink"><a>Click to expand...</a></div>
	</div>
</blockquote>I would love to go back. It would be much easier if we were
 equipped to travel in these regions and not lugging our house trough 
the jungle.<br>
<br>
I often think of these people, wonder how they are doing. But I have no means of contacting them.<br>
<br>
<br>

 feeling. I cannot describe it. We were in your country a few months

	</div>
</blockquote>Thanks for compliments. And that counts to everyone who is 
leaving comments here, it is really appreciated! We had tried a few 
times already to write down this story, but we always lost our 
motivation and it never got finished. Seeing that so many people are 
waiting for the next installment is just about the best motivation there
 is. Thank you Expedition Portal!  <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" class="smilie smilie--sprite smilie--sprite1" alt=":)" title="Smile    :)" data-shortname=":)"><br>

<blockquote class="bbCodeBlock bbCodeBlock--expandable bbCodeBlock--quote">
	
		<div class="bbCodeBlock-title">
			
				<a href="file:///forum/goto/post?id=746396" class="bbCodeBlock-sourceJump" data-xf-click="attribution" data-content-selector="#post-746396">PirateMcGee said:</a>
